    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

<span id="freeTextContainer13884089325705263793">A marriage in name only...<br/><br/>To save her family home, impulsive bookstore owner, Alexa Maria McKenzie, casts a love spell.   <span id="freeText13884089325705263793" style="display:none">A marriage in name only...<br /><br />To save her family home, impulsive bookstore owner, Alexa Maria McKenzie, casts a love spell. But she never planned on conjuring up her best friend's older brother—the powerful man who once shattered her heart.<br /><br />Billionaire Nicholas Ryan doesn’t believe in marriage, but in order to inherit his father’s corporation, he needs a wife and needs one fast. When he discovers his sister’s childhood friend is in dire financial straits, he offers Alexa a bold proposition.<br /><br />A marriage in name only with certain rules: Avoid entanglement. Keep things all business. Do not fall in love. The arrangement is only for a year so the rules shouldn’t be that hard to follow, right?<br /><br />Except fate has a way of upsetting the best-laid plans…</span>

<div id="review_300075625" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/300075625" />
    <a title="Jae" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3491949-jae"><img alt="Jae" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1551352235p2/3491949.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/300075625?book_show_action=true">Mar 24, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jae" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jae" href="/user/show/3491949-jae">Jae</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3491949-jae?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3491949-jae?shelf=hot-shagging-action">hot-shagging-action</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3491949-jae?shelf=2012">2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3491949-jae?shelf=silly-lol">silly-lol</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3491949-jae?shelf=5-star">5-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3491949-jae?shelf=first-read-by-author">first-read-by-author</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer300075625" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11867352600683197597">I have to admit, the hot cover was the first thing that drew me to the book. And was I glad that the content justified it. In spades.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379768906i/273032.jpg' width='540' height='310' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>It all started with her and his list of Mr/Ms Right.<br/><b>Hers :</b><br/>1) A Mets fan, <br/>2) loves books, art and poetry, <br/>3) believes in monogamy, <br/>4) wants children, <br/>5) knows how to communicate with a woman, <br/>6) loves animals, <br/>7) has a morale code of ethics and believes in honesty, <br/>8) a good lover <br/>9) has a strong sense of family, <br/>10) has $150,000 cash available.<br/><br/><b>His :</b><br/>1) a woman who d</span>
  <span id="freeText11867352600683197597" style="display:none">I have to admit, the hot cover was the first thing that drew me to the book. And was I glad that the content justified it. In spades.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379768906i/273032.jpg" width="540" height="310" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It all started with her and his list of Mr/Ms Right.<br><b>Hers :</b><br>1) A Mets fan, <br>2) loves books, art and poetry, <br>3) believes in monogamy, <br>4) wants children, <br>5) knows how to communicate with a woman, <br>6) loves animals, <br>7) has a morale code of ethics and believes in honesty, <br>8) a good lover <br>9) has a strong sense of family, <br>10) has $150,000 cash available.<br><br><b>His :</b><br>1) a woman who does not love me<br>2) a woman I do not desire to sleep with <br>3) a woman who does not have a big family<br>4) a woman who does not have any animals<br>5) a woman who does not want any children<br>6) a woman who has an independent career<br>7) a woman who will view the relationship as a business venture<br>8) a woman who is not overly emotional or impulsive<br>9) a woman I can trust<br><br>Alexa and Nicholas were both in deep trouble and the only solution was to get married. To. Each. Other. The thing was these two were old acquaintances and they had always rubbed each other wrong. Their constant head-on collisions were hilarious as well as sexual at times. <br><br>I loved their banters too,<br><i>She narrowed her eyes. "I see you're the same overbearing bully who teased me about my chest size. Some things don't change."<br>"I guess you're right. Some things remain the same. Others keep expanding."<br>She smiled, "and other things remain small."</i><br><br>The story was like any other typical marriage-in-name-only, but JP delivered it with her own writing style which combines hot-and-heavy with witty as well as sweet. A fun and enjoyable read. Can't wait for the next book about Alexa's BFF.</span>

<div id="review_364342529" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/364342529" />
    <a title="Katrina Passick Lumsden" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1964146-katrina-passick-lumsden"><img alt="Katrina Passick Lumsden" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1416959676p2/1964146.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/364342529?book_show_action=true">Jul 09, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katrina Passick Lumsden" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katrina Passick Lumsden" href="/user/show/1964146-katrina-passick-lumsden">Katrina Passick Lumsden</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/13497461-the-marriage-bargain">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer364342529" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12517941542630065642">*spoilers ahoy! Check yourself before you wreck yourself!*<br/><br/><br/><br/>..........................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................</span>
  <span id="freeText12517941542630065642" style="display:none">*spoilers ahoy! Check yourself before you wreck yourself!*<br><br><br><br>...................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................................I read that. Right? <br><br><a href="http://s1169.photobucket.com/albums/r512/shutterbird13/?action=view&amp;current=tumblr_ljv1ha48X61qg870qo1_250.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380383336ra/741518.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Yeah. Yeah, I did. I remember the story. What little there was, anyway. This book wasn't even a whole book, I don't think. It was somewhere between novel length and short story. Went by like <i>that</i>. It went by so quickly that I actually <i>forgot</i> I'd read a book. The next day, I was like, <i>Wait....didn't I read an entire book last night?</i> But you know, short as it was, it wasn't too terrible. It was tolerably written and had some genuinely funny bits. The female protagonist, Alexa, wasn't so bad. Sort of the antithesis of Ana Steele. Alexa was more like<br><br><a href="http://s1169.photobucket.com/albums/r512/shutterbird13/?action=view&amp;current=tumblr_m459vj1whg1roalwc.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380383336ra/741519.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I could get behind her no nonsense 'tude. I could. She was pretty cool. Then there was Nick. Here I have to shamefully admit that I've always had a soft spot for characters named Nick because it's my husband's name. Am I a silly quim? Hell yeah, but it's all good, I ain't hurtin' nobody. <br><br>Anyway, where the fuck was I? Oh, right, Nick. Well, on the outside, Nick is this cool, collected, cold hearted bastard who doesn't want love 'cause it's a myth and all that jazz, but underneath he's just all sad and lumpy. Like yogurt that's been left on the counter way too long. Only probably better looking. I <i>hope</i> better looking...<br><br>So, we already know the premise of the story; Alexa needs to marry for money, Nick needs to marry for money, so they decide to marry each other. For money. And then the inevitable happens. They fall in lust with each other<br><br><a href="http://s1169.photobucket.com/albums/r512/shutterbird13/?action=view&amp;current=tumblr_m227zkN9wg1rqadplo1_500.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380383336ra/741520.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>then they fall in <i>lurve</i> with each other, then all hell breaks loose when Alexa gets knocked up with Nick's baby and he freaks out, insisting Alexa only got pregnant to "trap him". Yes, Nick is a bit full of himself. Anyway, the whole thing is so predictable, you know where it goes from there. Yes, there's a HEA ending, and yes, Nick comes to his senses, and yes, there's a sad adopted dog involved. <br><br><a href="http://s1169.photobucket.com/albums/r512/shutterbird13/?action=view&amp;current=tumblr_m07tjyceNf1qihf5r.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380383337ra/741521.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Psst! The dog is a metaphor for Nick. If I were Nick, I'd be highly insulted. But then, I'd be a rich architect, so I probably wouldn't really care. <br><br>The ending is so romance fiction typical. He shows up at a poetry reading and does the whole eating-of-his-pride thing, and is all like<br><br><a href="http://s1169.photobucket.com/albums/r512/shutterbird13/?action=view&amp;current=tumblr_m5n7xuO8Tt1r9jhwp.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380383337ra/741522.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>and Alexa, all pregnant and mopey, is just all tears and love and gag-me-with-sugar sentimental. There's a group hug. The end. <br><br>It was hokey and predictable and cheesy and character development be damned, but you know what?<br><br><a href="http://s1169.photobucket.com/albums/r512/shutterbird13/?action=view&amp;current=tumblr_lpio3zWkgZ1qgqauu.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380383337ra/741523.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="12517941542630065642" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer297419818" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15918012249275821035">Almost a DNF. I came soooooo close to chucking this one, but I skimmed the last third of the book as I did want to finish. Overall this was a very underwhelming read. I love a great contemporary romance with steam, but this was too formulaic and lacked a decent story to keep me interested. The plot was just downright boring. I do like a marriage of convenience plot, but this was just too hokey as they keep going back and forth on their desires for sex. The heroine's need to lie was baffling, and</span>
  <span id="freeText15918012249275821035" style="display:none">Almost a DNF. I came soooooo close to chucking this one, but I skimmed the last third of the book as I did want to finish. Overall this was a very underwhelming read. I love a great contemporary romance with steam, but this was too formulaic and lacked a decent story to keep me interested. The plot was just downright boring. I do like a marriage of convenience plot, but this was just too hokey as they keep going back and forth on their desires for sex. The heroine's need to lie was baffling, and the heroes sudden change of heart is a plot device so often found in bad fiction. While it had the occasional cute moments, I can't recommend this one, sorry. </span>

<div id="review_280090383" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/280090383" />
    <a title="MBR" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4201191-mbr"><img alt="MBR" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1586514075p2/4201191.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/280090383?book_show_action=true">Feb 18, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="MBR" class="user" itemprop="url" name="MBR" href="/user/show/4201191-mbr">MBR</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of marriage of convenience theme, fans of Jennifer Probst, Everyone who LOVES romances!</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4201191-mbr?shelf=haunted-by-the-past-hero">haunted-by-the-past-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4201191-mbr?shelf=protective-hero">protective-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4201191-mbr?shelf=angsty-read">angsty-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4201191-mbr?shelf=brooding-hero">brooding-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4201191-mbr?shelf=emotional-wrangler">emotional-wrangler</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4201191-mbr?shelf=hottest-first-kiss">hottest-first-kiss</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4201191-mbr?shelf=shared-past">shared-past</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4201191-mbr?shelf=sizzling-sexual-tension">sizzling-sexual-tension</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4201191-mbr?shelf=commitment-phobic-hero">commitment-phobic-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4201191-mbr?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer280090383" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8297663299028401495">All romance lovers out there, make way for the superbly talented Jennifer Probst who has succeeded in earning herself an auto-buy spot on my already long list of authors whose books I wouldn’t hesitate to purchase. Not only do I immediately purchase Jennifer Probst’s books, but I stop everything I am reading at the moment and plunge into her books with an enthusiasm that tells a story of its own.<br/><br/>27 year old Alexandria Maria McKenzie (Alexa) is in a bit of a dilemma. She needs a husband, preferab</span>
  <span id="freeText8297663299028401495" style="display:none">All romance lovers out there, make way for the superbly talented Jennifer Probst who has succeeded in earning herself an auto-buy spot on my already long list of authors whose books I wouldn’t hesitate to purchase. Not only do I immediately purchase Jennifer Probst’s books, but I stop everything I am reading at the moment and plunge into her books with an enthusiasm that tells a story of its own.<br /><br />27 year old Alexandria Maria McKenzie (Alexa) is in a bit of a dilemma. She needs a husband, preferably with $150,000 to spare and she needs it fast. Brushing aside her ideals and her image of the perfect husband to share her life with isn’t easy for Alexa. But she will do it because she is willing to do everything in her power to rescue her family home. And so Alexa casts a little love spell, all the while feeling a bit silly but nevertheless hopeful that Mother Earth would send her way, a man who would meet all those qualities that she wants in a man together with that wad of cold hard cash to give as well.<br /><br />30 year old Nicholas Ryan (Nick) is in a bit of a fix as well. Nick has a fortune at his fingertips, but his Uncle Earl had changed all the rules of the game at the last minute and left him hanging. His dream of owning Dreamscape, the architectural firm that brings out all his emotions and creativity in one stride would belong to him, only if gets married before the stated time is up. Nick is a man who doesn’t believe in happily ever afters, large families and the strength of a love between two people that defies all odds and logic. And he is certainly the direct opposite of what Alexa envisions as a husband for herself and nor is he too thrilled to know that his only viable option of a wife for a year is none other than his childhood tormentor Alexa herself.<br /><br />14 year since that humiliating experience that had broken Alexa’s heart, she meets an altogether more controlled and formidable Nick, whose cold and hard way of looking at a marriage leaves a lot to be desired. But Alexa is desperate enough and thus she enters into a bargain which would give them both a marriage in name only, merely a business transaction on both sides, cold and aloof right from the onset until the 1 year period is up and both parties go their separate ways. But neither Alexa nor Nick thinks of those messier emotions that could botch things up, or those tendrils of desire that slowly erupts, leaving them both wanting more and brings in the possibility of that elusive thing called love that could last a lifetime.<br /><br />Jennifer Probst surprised me with The Marriage Bargain. I was already in high anticipatory mode when I started on the book, knowing that Jennifer would not disappoint me. What surprised me, and all in a good way I must add, was the thread of humor that was introduced into the book right from the very beginning. Humor and red hot passion is an unbeatable combination in any romance novel and I was a goner from the first chapter itself.<br /><br />Alexa was a character I loved right from the very beginning. Her sense of humor, her loyalty and kindness, the way that she gives everything she has got with no expectations of gaining anything back in return were some of those traits that drew me towards her in the same way way that Nick continued to be as the story progressed. Alexa is a woman who is comfortable with who she is, a woman who is helplessly drawn towards her husband as she had been when she was much younger and more naive, already in love with a man who had no illusions about love and happily ever afters. And Alexa’s well rounded family certainly makes for a heartwarming addition to an already character driven story that proved to be of the unputdownable kind. <br /><br />Nick *sigh*, Nick is a character I am going to be remembering for a long, long time. He is a man torn between the desire he feels for his altogether too alluring for her own good wife, a woman who confuses and befuddles him as no other woman ever has and his need for control that remains to be a thing of the past when Alexa steps into his life. He has no intention of staying around after the one year period is up to see where their relationship could go, already convinced that he would never make a good husband, a conviction born out of a childhood that had seen the endless battles of war waged between his parents.<br /><br />The sexual tension that Jennifer so cleverly weaves into the story is of the scorching variety, the tingles and jolts that the reader experiences right along with Nick and Alexa one of the best parts of the story. Jennifer has a talent for building up the tension until it is an either do or die impasse that the characters reach, and the reader cannot help but be drawn towards the magic that unfolds that just left my throat parched, in dire need of a cool, tall glass of iced water to smooth things over. Without gushing further on this aspect, I will just let my quotes section do it for you.<br /><br />And don’t let me forget the verbal warfare between Nick and Alexa, Nick finally meeting his match in every way. A woman who doesn’t back down, a woman who brings those little bits of color to his otherwise stark and empty life, showing Nick that life as he had known it is no longer an option for him. It is Alexa’s patience when it comes to Nick, the way she draws the inner soul inside of him that years to embrace those emotions which Nick is afraid to name that just makes this one of the best romances I have read in a long while.<br /><br />A passion that is explosive as the love that unfolds is tender, a beautiful happily ever after that encompasses everything; Jennifer Probst delivers a fiery and wild romance that goes straight to your heart.<br /><br />Highly recommended!<br /><br /><b> Rating=5/5</b><br /><br />An outstanding 5-Star Read! Loved this.<br /><br />Quotes included below!</span>
  <a data-text-id="8297663299028401495" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3161105-maida---v--"><img alt="Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1555353893p2/3161105.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/289283559?book_show_action=true">Mar 05, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»" href="/user/show/3161105-maida---v--">Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=signed-paperback-hc-i-own">signed-paperback-hc-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=paperback-or-hc-i-own">paperback-or-hc-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer289283559" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6235673220906364271">I LOVED THIS BOOK!!! It was sweet, funny, fresh, fun and very engaging. A truly sweet romance. I loved everything about it except for the fact....IT WAS TOOO SHORT!!! :( I really hate it when that happens...the best stories are always the short ones..WHY OH WHY!!?? I could have easily read about Nick and Alexa for a long time.....like oh I don’t know 500 or 600 pages more!! I loved the story and the romance. This book totally brought on my girly-girl....and I couldn’t help but swoon and drool...</span>
  <span id="freeText6235673220906364271" style="display:none">I LOVED THIS BOOK!!! It was sweet, funny, fresh, fun and very engaging. A truly sweet romance. I loved everything about it except for the fact....IT WAS TOOO SHORT!!! :( I really hate it when that happens...the best stories are always the short ones..WHY OH WHY!!?? I could have easily read about Nick and Alexa for a long time.....like oh I don’t know 500 or 600 pages more!! I loved the story and the romance. This book totally brought on my girly-girl....and I couldn’t help but swoon and drool...yes drool over Nick! What a hottie!<br /><br />The most hilarious part I can’t help but laugh every time I read it:<br /><br />She narrowed her eyes. “I see you’re the same overbearing bully who teased me about my chest size. Some things don’t change.” <br />He focused his attention on the dip of her dress. “I guess you’re right. Some things remain the same. Others keep expanding.” <br />Her breath caught at the jab, but she surprised him when she smiled. “And other things remain small.” Her pointed stare settled directly on the bulge in the center of his pants.<br /><br />LMFAO.....that had me laughing for a good 15 minutes!!! In fact Alexa and Nick’s relationship is full of laughter, sweet moments, hot sexy moments (of course.. ;p), love, and one hell of an emotional roller coaster ride! It was fantastic! I loved how their relationship grows over the course of the story and eventually helps both the main characters overcome their life obstacles. They both found comfort in each other....and they truly were meant to be together!! I AM COMPLETELY IN LOVE!!! Their romance is hot, it’s steamy and yeah it gets you hot and bothered....but that was the best part...waiting to see who gave up first! There is plenty of heat and attraction...to keep you right at the edge of your seat! YUM YUM YUMMY!!! =)<br /><br />Alexa was hilarious, beautiful, witty, sassy, and a strong female character. I loved her easy going personality and her knack to annoy the hell out of Nick when she felt like it! LOL ;p The most amazing thing I admired about Alexa was that she never goes back on her word....and always keeps her promises and never gives up. It was admirable and it was one of her best qualities!<br /><br />Nick....well first things first....THIS GUY IS HOT...AS IN HOT AS HELL HOT!!! YEAH THAT’S RIGHT.....just let your imaginations run wild ladies!!! I also loved Nick. Although, he was insecure about many things especially when it came to claiming a wife or having children, he was still a very determined person to make everything work out between him and Alexa....and really that’s all someone can ask for! Right from the beginning you see that he is attracted to Alexa but his feelings don’t have any depth....however through the course of the story...you get to not only see Nick’s feelings evolve but you also get to see him grow as a person! It was simply....PERFECT!!<br /><br />Overall, this was a fantastic book and I really can’t find any flaws...and even if there were any...I wouldn’t have noticed cause I was so hooked to the story....I read this all in one freakin day!!!! That’s how much I loved it and couldn’t put it down! I was very glad to see Nick and Alexa work out their kinks in their relationship and finally end up together! And the way Nick won Alexa’s heart...*swoon* I nearly cried at all the wonderful, and heart felt comments he said wearing a METTS JERSEY [he’s a Yankees fan...and to win Alexa heart he wore her fav teams outfit]!!!! What a charmer and heart steeler!! I wouldn’t mind a man like Nick! LOL ;p I can’t wait to read the next installment, The Marriage Trap. This will be Maggie and the Count’s story and I CANNOT wait to read this one! Maggie was such a sassy character....and the Count was just PURE HOT ITALIAN MAN...YUMMY!! This will be something to read about...hopefully its funny as hell! ;p <br /><br />Ms. Probst you did a fantastic job...and completely have me hooked with your work....just hurry up with the next book.....please *smiles sweetly*! =)<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6235673220906364271" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText9737181043591621785" style="display:none">Spoiler Free Review<b> -Quick Review</b><br />4 STARS out of 5<br />Genre: Contemporary romance<br /><i><br />Alexa squirmed in her seat as the silence in the BMW stretched between them. Her husband-to-be seemed just as uncomfortable, he chose to focus his energy into his MP3 player. She tried not to wince when he settled on Mozart. He actually enjoyed music without words. She almost shuddered again when she though of sharing a residence with him. For. An. Entire. Year.</i><b><br />"Do you have any Black Eye Peas?"</b><i><br />He looked puzzled by the question.</i><b>"To eat?"</b><i><br />She held back a groan.</i><b> "I'll even settle for some of the old classics Sinatra, Bennett, Martin."</b><i><br />He remained silent.</i><b><br />"Eagles? Beatles? Just yell if any of these names sound familiar."</b><i><br />His shoulder stiffen.</i><b> "I know who they are. Would you prefer Beethoven?"</b><br />~Alexa and Nick<br /><br />Hahahahahahaha! This guy?! These two had me bent over laughing at their banter and their antics.<br /><br />Nicholas Ryan is a billionaire looking for a wife so that he can fulfill a requirement made in his uncle's will. By doing so he can have complete control of the family business. The will states he must be married for at least a year. No problem right? Thing is he does not want to marry his supermodel girlfriend Gabriela, he senses that she is falling in love with him. And he does not do long term. So, she is off the list without even knowing why. And she is none to happy about it either.<br /><br />Alexa McKenzie needs one-hundred and fifty thousand dollars cash in order to save her parents home. And she needs the money<i> NOW.</i> Nick may not be at the top of her list when it comes to what she is looking for in a man. But his bank account is.<br /><br />These two come together making a deal that should settle both of their problems. And it does. They just never expected to fall in love in the process. <br /><br /><u>Thoughts</u><br />This was a fun quick read filled with plenty of witty banter as well as some steamy love sessions. I totally recommend this book to romance lovers who enjoy a nice balance of steam and laughter. The hero has some mommy and daddy issues but the author chose not to delve in too deep. Making this a light fun read. <b><br />Check it out!! </b><br /><br />My Ratings<br />Characters- Lovable and Witty<br />Writing Style- Good<br />Plot/Storyline- Good<br />Steam Factor- Medium/Moderately Steamy<br />Overall- I liked it! Check it out!!<b><br /><br />Now go forth and read, Then come tell us about it on Goodreads!</b><br /><br />For more reviews go to <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogspot.com">http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogs...</a> </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11289096517312763200">I really enjoyed this one! So much so that I have a ton of funny quips and scenes highlighted on my eReader.<br/> <br/>In <b>The Marriage Bargain</b> two childhood “friends” (and I use that term loosely), agree to enter into a marriage of convenience. Nick needs a wife as a condition to inherit some cash, and Alexa is willing to accept the terms of the bargain for a small payout of her own to help save her family’s home. When their contract requirements begin to collide, sparks start to fly and Nick and Alexa fi</span>
  <span id="freeText11289096517312763200" style="display:none">I really enjoyed this one! So much so that I have a ton of funny quips and scenes highlighted on my eReader.<br /> <br />In <b>The Marriage Bargain</b> two childhood “friends” (and I use that term loosely), agree to enter into a marriage of convenience. Nick needs a wife as a condition to inherit some cash, and Alexa is willing to accept the terms of the bargain for a small payout of her own to help save her family’s home. When their contract requirements begin to collide, sparks start to fly and Nick and Alexa find that this marriage bargain is turning into something they didn’t expect.<br /><br />Okay, let me just say… yes there’s an element of predictability to this story. I knew how it was going to end, but in all fairness when you go into a story expecting something light, romantic, funny and fulfilling that’s the perfect type of predictability an author can deliver. Jennifer Probst did a great job of blending her protags to create a perfect pair that were funny and quite entertaining.<br /><br />So, if you’re looking for a moment of reality suspension with an ending that leaves you smiling <b>The Marriage Bargain</b> is the perfect choice <br /></span>

<div id="review_290828931" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/290828931" />

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/290828931?book_show_action=true">Mar 08, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Leslie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Leslie" href="/user/show/5433591-leslie">Leslie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5433591-leslie?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5433591-leslie?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5433591-leslie?shelf=hilarious">hilarious</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5433591-leslie?shelf=chicklit">chicklit</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer290828931" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17110114731830912144">An incredibly fun, light, humorous and sexy read! <br/><br/>Nick needs a wife. His late uncle makes sure of that, too as details are revealed in his will. There is a set timeline for Nick to marry, which will grant him his uncle's wealth, and we're talking millions, upon his death. Trouble is, Nick comes from a broken family with enormous dysfunctional luggage, and even though he's capable of loving women, he dosen't ever see himself falling "in love" with a any woman, much less having a family.<br/><br/>Alexa is N</span>
  <span id="freeText17110114731830912144" style="display:none">An incredibly fun, light, humorous and sexy read! <br /><br />Nick needs a wife. His late uncle makes sure of that, too as details are revealed in his will. There is a set timeline for Nick to marry, which will grant him his uncle's wealth, and we're talking millions, upon his death. Trouble is, Nick comes from a broken family with enormous dysfunctional luggage, and even though he's capable of loving women, he dosen't ever see himself falling "in love" with a any woman, much less having a family.<br /><br />Alexa is Nick's sister's best friend. She grew up with Maggie and Nick and knows a thing or two about his family and Nick, personally. Alexa also had a major crush on him all those years ago when they dated for a short time in their teens. When Alexa's parents begin showing signs of serious money problems, she is determined to help them save their beloved home any way she can. It wasn't hard for Maggie to devise a plan to help out her brother and Alexa's desperate family; all in one easy transaction: <i>Alexa will marry Nick...immediately.</i> Seems simple enough, right? Yep, you would be mistaken. <br /><br />Even though this story was predictable, the author's storytelling kept me thorougly interested and made me excited to get back to Nick and Alexa every chance I got! That says a lot about how this book was written. The reader is never in doubt as to what's going on in his or her head, (that's the beauty of 3rd person, if executed correctly), and I understood their fears, doubts and surging passion even more as the story continued. Oh, and the passion is <b>REALLY GREAT</b> and well timed. I was, however, slightly disappointed by the ending since it felt rushed and a tad unrealistic; although, didn't sway how much I still enjoyed the book as a whole. This is another great example of a book to grab if you're about to hop a plane or in need of a little rainy-day escape! <br /><br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17110114731830912144" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer6771584551683102898"><b>2,5 stars</b><br/><br/><b>The reason for reading:</b> Wanted something short and light.<br/><br/><b>Worth the experince?:</b> <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419878119ra/13143703.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Eh...       <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer290389217" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17653308057014678876">I loved this one! This was such a fast, entertaining, and sexy read. <br/><br/>Nick and Alexa were childhood friends, but hurt over adolescent stupidity, drove them apart. Alexa is still best friends with Nick's sister, Maggie, and this is how Alexa and Nick end up together again in a business arrangement. Nick needs a wife quick, to fulfill conditions in a will, and Alexa needs money quick, to bail her parents out of debt, so they won't lose the family home. Nick doesn’t want a real wife, he feels he cou</span>
  <span id="freeText17653308057014678876" style="display:none">I loved this one! This was such a fast, entertaining, and sexy read. <br /><br />Nick and Alexa were childhood friends, but hurt over adolescent stupidity, drove them apart. Alexa is still best friends with Nick's sister, Maggie, and this is how Alexa and Nick end up together again in a business arrangement. Nick needs a wife quick, to fulfill conditions in a will, and Alexa needs money quick, to bail her parents out of debt, so they won't lose the family home. Nick doesn’t want a real wife, he feels he could never love someone properly, and doesn't ever want to be a father. He's experienced the pain they can bring, first-hand, and so he'd rather pay someone, than commit to a real marriage. So Nick and Alexa sign a contract, and enter in this marriage bargain/business arrangement, that is to last a year. <br /><br />Yes, the plot is a bit predictable, and there are no life-lessons learned, but it's well-paced, and so much fun, you don't care. There are lots of hilarious moments, stemming from the antagonistic relationship between Alexa and Nick. The scene with the dogs was priceless! This had me laughing:<br /><br /><i>
  <b>For a few seconds, he convinced himself he was having a dream, and would wake up in his own bed. Then he realized the scene was real. And a murder would be committed. Involving his wife. The room was in shambles. Shredded papers flew in every direction. The luxurious carpet was mottled with liquid circles that didn't look like water………Nick closed his eyes. Counted to three. Opened them. Then screamed his wife's name at the top of his lungs.</b>
</i><br /><br />These two revert back to their teenage relationship, of torturing each other many times, and you can't help but laugh at their juvenile behavior. There's a lot of passion, and feeling between these two, as they manage to press each other's buttons, which often leads to losing control, and some pretty spicy scenes *fans self*! This one put the Smut, in Smut Monday! Another great pick. <br /></span>

<div id="review_2125376540" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2125376540" />
    <a title="Jacob Proffitt" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1331641-jacob-proffitt"><img alt="Jacob Proffitt" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1325699498p2/1331641.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2125376540?book_show_action=true">Sep 15, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacob Proffitt" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacob Proffitt" href="/user/show/1331641-jacob-proffitt">Jacob Proffitt</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/13497461-the-marriage-bargain">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1331641-jacob-proffitt?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1331641-jacob-proffitt?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1331641-jacob-proffitt?shelf=unfinished">unfinished</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2125376540" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18132717763919044947">I made it almost all the way through this before my loathing for Nick finally overcame my desire to see Alexa happy. And it's not so much that Nick is a jerk and completely unworthy of her attention (though he is those things). It's that he doesn't make any sense in a tropey way that I wish authors would stop trying to make work. Let me lay it out in explicit terms. If a guy prides himself on rational analysis, then he can't possibly believe the truly stupid propositions that love doesn't exist </span>
  <span id="freeText18132717763919044947" style="display:none">I made it almost all the way through this before my loathing for Nick finally overcame my desire to see Alexa happy. And it's not so much that Nick is a jerk and completely unworthy of her attention (though he is those things). It's that he doesn't make any sense in a tropey way that I wish authors would stop trying to make work. Let me lay it out in explicit terms. If a guy prides himself on rational analysis, then he can't possibly believe the truly stupid propositions that love doesn't exist and that monogamy is an illusion. Those beliefs make him a self-involved idiot who couldn't analyze his way past a sleeping toddler.<br /><br />The capper happened when Nick's father breezes in, has a single conversation, spouting self-involved, moronic things and Nick swallows it down hook, line, and sinker. The dad who is an indolent jerk who can't be bothered to pay attention to Nick must <em>of course</em> hold the keys to Nick's future. Authors, this makes Nick a complete and utter moron and going from that to hurting Alexa makes him the giantest douchnozzle that ever nozzed. Probst spends the length of the story spouting nonsense about Nick being smart and rational but <em>showing him</em> being a dramatic idiot ruled by his hormones and with an inability to weigh simple facts to reach obvious conclusions (like, for example, that his father is a selfish jerk whose every word about relationships should be disregarded as the empty wind it obviously is).<br /><br />Also, Probst overwrites something terrible. The one that hangs in my memory is Alexa lamenting damage to her "mental sanity". As opposed to her, er, physical . . . sanity ?</span>
  <a data-text-id="18132717763919044947" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_305191037" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/305191037" />
    <a title="Rachel (BAVR)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6303796-rachel-bavr"><img alt="Rachel (BAVR)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1396635700p2/6303796.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/305191037?book_show_action=true">Apr 02, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel (BAVR)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel (BAVR)" href="/user/show/6303796-rachel-bavr">Rachel (BAVR)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6303796-rachel-bavr?shelf=angst-city">angst-city</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6303796-rachel-bavr?shelf=worst-person-ever-hero">worst-person-ever-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6303796-rachel-bavr?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6303796-rachel-bavr?shelf=doormat-heroine">doormat-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6303796-rachel-bavr?shelf=brooding-mcbroody-hero">brooding-mcbroody-hero</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer305191037" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13704878345650127628">I actually enjoyed reading this book because it was such an easy read. But full disclaimer ahead: I did not appreciate the storyline AT ALL, and my review will devolve into my problems with creativity in the romance market and the hero that I didn't like at all. Read on if you're prepared for the snark.<br/><br/>I've read this wangst before. Emotionally Stunted Super Douche enters a marriage of convenience with teh evulz womanz, falls in insta-lust, gets emotionally involved, and then loses his damn mind.</span>
  <span id="freeText13704878345650127628" style="display:none">I actually enjoyed reading this book because it was such an easy read. But full disclaimer ahead: I did not appreciate the storyline AT ALL, and my review will devolve into my problems with creativity in the romance market and the hero that I didn't like at all. Read on if you're prepared for the snark.<br><br>I've read this wangst before. Emotionally Stunted Super Douche enters a marriage of convenience with teh evulz womanz, falls in insta-lust, gets emotionally involved, and then loses his damn mind. During his big, life-changing revelation, we get this: <i>"He was a gutless coward who hurt people because he only cared about himself."</i> Well, <b>yeah</b>! That's why the heroine <i>shouldn't</i> have married the bastard in the first place. Ladies, a brief moment of honesty here. No man will transform from a gutless coward who hurts people into freaking husband of the year at the turn of a dime. No woman will, either. People's personalities <b>aren't built that way</b>. And sure, I can deal with reading this story once, but it's like this is the only story contemporary and historical authors have to tell. It's 2012, right? At this rate, I'll be reading the <b>same freaking story</b> in a nursing home in 2082 (I plan to live for a long time), only with probably robotic penises and spaceship honeymoons. <br><br>In the spirit of fairness, I can't criticize <i>The Marriage Bargain</i> for being exactly what every other romance is. But wait! I paid for this book, so yes I can! In this day and age, I just thought that women had evolved beyond these "all women fall in love with assholes with daddy issues who emotionally berate them until they can think of no better thing than having their babies" tragedies. Or at the very least, I thought we had added some variety to our fantasies. But nope. This story makes no attempt at distinguishing itself in the market. This plot is like the tapioca pudding of the romance genre. On the bright side, it was a fast read! <br><br>Meet Nick GotLotsaMoney, an emotionally stunted asshat who's supposed to look like this:<br><br><a href="http://gifsoup.com/view/2904298/your-soul.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br><a href="http://gifsoup.com/" title="GIFSoup" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">GIFSoup</a><br><br>But gives the impression of this:<br><br><a href="http://gifsoup.com/view/32913/baby.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br><a href="http://gifsoup.com/" title="GIFSoup" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">GIFSoup</a><br><br>He has to marry and stay married for a whole year (OMG!) to claim his full inheritance because his dead uncle said so. But BIG PROBLEM. Nick hates relationships, marriage, babies, emotional stability, and holidays. He pretty much hates women, too, because they're all lying liars with expectations and other evil stuff who like to trap men in marriages with BABIES. Naturally, Nick goes in search of the perfect Stepford Wife to fill his bank account. He writes this hilarious list of requirements for his soon-to-be bride captive:<br><br>(Just imagine all the internal wangsting that happened to create a monster of this magnitude.)<br><i> A woman who does not love me.<br>A woman I do not desire to sleep with.<br>A woman who does not have a big family.<br>A woman who does not have any animals.<br>A woman who does not want any children.<br>A woman who has an independent career.<br>A woman who will view the relationship as a business venture.<br>A woman who is not overly emotional or impulsive.<br>A woman I can trust.</i><br><br>I'm assuming that, "A woman who only breathes three times a day" and "A woman who never uses the bathroom" were cut on the editing room floor to save for word space. So clearly, Nick is emotionally damaged. His parents got a divorce, and his dad is an Asshat Scholar. Instead of growing beyond that, Nick has decided to die a little more inside every day and make every person who cares for him miserable. Because THAT'S a reasonable reaction. So who on earth can fix this pathetic lump of twagedy? <br><br>Meet Alexa PluckyButPoor! She's basically a Disney Princess, only SEXY. <br><br><a href="http://gifsoup.com/view/1441990/rapunzel.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br><a href="http://gifsoup.com/" title="GIFSoup" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">GIFSoup</a><br><i>Pictured: A million times too good for Nick.</i><br><br>Alexa owns a bookstore and can barely pay the bills. She's free-spirited and impulsive! She freaking LOVES animals so much that she adopts bundles of them from the humane society. Alexa's heart is so damn big that her chest probably doesn't have room for her lungs anymore. Her best friend is Nick's sister, and Alexa is desperate. Apparently, the only way she can pay off her parents' mortgage that they can't afford is to marry a douchey rich dude. Despite the fact that Nick broke her heart when she was 14, Alexa takes the plunge and marries the pathetic billionaire. <br><br>Blah, blah, blah. They fight! Blah, blah, blah. Steamy kiss! Blah, blah, blah. Nick rejects Alexa because of all the feelings he's feeling. Repeat. <br><br>Naturally, their marriage ruse gets all complicated because they're actually meant for each other. So the final quarter of the book is one long death march toward Nick's ultimate destruction of all things happy. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Alexa ends up pregant due to a birth control malfunction. Instead of dealing with it like a reasonable adult, Nick goes on the advice of his horrible father who he HATES WITH A VISCERAL PASSION and decides that Alexa planned the pregnancy to trap him and all of his pwecious money. That's all women know how to do, in Nick's mind: trap men and get pregnant. We're very fearsome creatures, right? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Yes, I'm a grumpy goose. The book wasn't bad. It delivered exactly what it promised. Unfortunately, I am just about UP TO HERE with the story. Why are we glorifying men like Nick in 2012? Do authors not realize that men can be sexy alphas without acting like pretentious sexist douchebags? Sorry, Romancelandia. Some of these tropes are getting TIRED. </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="13704878345650127628" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_286612072" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/286612072" />
    <a title="Hazel *Craves the Angst Reviews*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6848917-hazel-craves-the-angst-reviews"><img alt="Hazel *Craves the Angst Reviews*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1381252112p2/6848917.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/286612072?book_show_action=true">Mar 01, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Hazel *Craves the Angst Reviews*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Hazel *Craves the Angst Reviews*" href="/user/show/6848917-hazel-craves-the-angst-reviews">Hazel *Craves the Angst Reviews*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">romance readers</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6848917-hazel-craves-the-angst-reviews?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6848917-hazel-craves-the-angst-reviews?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer286612072" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15525844363705087996"><u>The Marriage Bargain</u> is a romance novel by <i>Jennifer Probst</i>. I was in B&N one day and looking through their "read in store" selections and found this title. I like the occasional romance and decided to give it a try with the one hour read for free that B&N offers for their Nook customers. I instantly fell in love with this story. I hadn't even read for the full hour yet, was only 20 pages in before I decided to purchase it and continue on! <br/><br/>This is the typical romance novel where the motivation fo</span>
  <span id="freeText15525844363705087996" style="display:none"><u>The Marriage Bargain</u> is a romance novel by <i>Jennifer Probst</i>. I was in B&amp;N one day and looking through their "read in store" selections and found this title. I like the occasional romance and decided to give it a try with the one hour read for free that B&amp;N offers for their Nook customers. I instantly fell in love with this story. I hadn't even read for the full hour yet, was only 20 pages in before I decided to purchase it and continue on! <br /><br />This is the typical romance novel where the motivation for coming together is money. Nick needs a wife to claim his deceased Uncle's business and Alexa needs money to rescue her family's home. They reluctantly come together to serve each others purpose and the attraction is instant. But what makes this novel different from most is its quirky, fun and exciting ride from the first page to the last! Nick is smoldering hot and watching his inimical walls crumble was intriguing! Alexa is beatnik and her antics are amusing. I laughed out loud at many of the ridiculous scenes. And I can always count it as a win when I get the butterfly's from reading the pull-tug between two opposing forces. This was just a truly excellent and fun read.</span>

          </span>

<div id="review_286079876" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/286079876" />
    <a title="Beate" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/407744-beate"><img alt="Beate" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1370358192p2/407744.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/286079876?book_show_action=true">Feb 29, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beate" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beate" href="/user/show/407744-beate">Beate</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/13497461-the-marriage-bargain">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/407744-beate?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/407744-beate?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer286079876" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9353533840860199483">This book right here is the reason why I'm so willing to give small press and selfpublishing a chance. This book right here is the reason why I so patiently roam <i>Amazon</i> and <i>Goodreads,</i> looking for new and undiscovered authors, why I put up with a lot of really bad books in the hopes they will lead me to something like this.<br/><br/><i>The Marriage Bargain</i> is a good romance book. The kind that is hard to find these days. Most books that hide under the <i>Romance</i> banner are erotica books in disguise. So finding s</span>
  <span id="freeText9353533840860199483" style="display:none">This book right here is the reason why I'm so willing to give small press and selfpublishing a chance. This book right here is the reason why I so patiently roam <i>Amazon</i> and <i>Goodreads,</i> looking for new and undiscovered authors, why I put up with a lot of really bad books in the hopes they will lead me to something like this.<br /><br /><i>The Marriage Bargain</i> is a good romance book. The kind that is hard to find these days. Most books that hide under the <i>Romance</i> banner are erotica books in disguise. So finding something that is what I call a true romance book...well...it feels like I found a precious gem.<br /><br />More often than not, romance books dive right into bed with the characters, and from then on it feels like you're in a sex-marathon. Oh the authors do try to weave in a plot of some kind, but too often if falls flat.<br /><br />In <i>The Marriage Bargain</i> the UST (unresolved sexual tension) is so heavy it makes you want to grab the characters and shake them until they come to their senses. I love that we have to get through more than half the book before anything more than heavy makeout sessions happen. Best of all, none of their sexual encounters are too graphic. A lot is left to the reader's imagination. Honestly, there is nothing sexier than that. Erotica has its time and place, but a true romance is always a win.<br /><br />Speaking of romance, I love that the questions about love aren't resolved until the very end of the book. There are no boring moments that make you reach out for another book to read. Ms Probst spins a tale that makes it impossible to put the book down. And yes, I'll manage just fine on only 3 hours of sleep... :D<br /><br />I have browsed by this book many, many times. The reason why I didn't stop by this book until now, is the cover. It's a gorgeous picture, so it's not that. But I just don't like it as a book-cover. I find it offputting. I like to find out for myself through reading what the characters look like, and a cover like that gets in the way of that. But it kept on popping up on my browsing through Amazon books, so I caved and read the blurb. The blurb is what was the real seller for me.<br /><br />Thanks to a very good summary, I picked up this book. And annoyance over cover aside, I'm exstatic I've read this.<br /><br />Even if you're like me, and none too crazy about the cover, read the blurb, then read the book. If you're tired of all the marathon-sex that most books seem to be full of, pick up this one. This is a feel-good book. Snuggle up in front of a fire, with a hot coffee, tea, or cocoa, and escape into the world of Ms Probst. You won't regret it.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9353533840860199483" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_292024676" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/292024676" />
    <a title="Anne OK" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/285610-anne-ok"><img alt="Anne OK" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505981069p2/285610.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/292024676?book_show_action=true">Mar 10, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anne OK" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anne OK" href="/user/show/285610-anne-ok">Anne OK</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/285610-anne-ok?shelf=2012-reads">2012-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer292024676" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13370933419249958678">This delightfully captivating book is written by a new-to-me-author. Simply put, this was just what the doctor ordered. I had such fun reading Jennifer Probst’s “The Marriage Bargain.” <br/><br/>Both characters stole my heart from the very start. Each had a major problem requiring a quick fix. Alexa needs money to save her family’s home from foreclosure. Nick needs a wife to fulfill the conditions set forth in his uncle’s will allowing him to inherit full control of his family’s business. If she’ll be his</span>
  <span id="freeText13370933419249958678" style="display:none">This delightfully captivating book is written by a new-to-me-author. Simply put, this was just what the doctor ordered. I had such fun reading Jennifer Probst’s “The Marriage Bargain.” <br /><br />Both characters stole my heart from the very start. Each had a major problem requiring a quick fix. Alexa needs money to save her family’s home from foreclosure. Nick needs a wife to fulfill the conditions set forth in his uncle’s will allowing him to inherit full control of his family’s business. If she’ll be his wife for one year, he’ll give her the money she needs. It’s supposed to be a simple contract between the two of them. No emotional commitments. No entanglements. Just follow the rules and everyone gets what they need and no one will be any the wiser. Right? <br /><br />“Oh what a tangled web we weave when first we practice to deceive!” <br /><br />Alexa McKenzie and Nick Ryan’s “marriage in name only” story is absolutely perfect for readers looking for a healthy dose of romance. It’s well written and full of sexual heat and witty dialogue. I absolutely loved “The Marriage Bargain” and I'm looking forward to reading more of Jennifer Probst’s books! Highly recommend. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13370933419249958678" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1006034498925409860">This is a fun, sexy read that I enjoyed...<b>3.5 stars</b><br/><br/>Jennifer Probst took the Marriage of Convenience plot and with her witty dialog, the strong build of sexual tension and finally those hot love scenes and made this a winner. <br/><br/>Nick Ryan doesn't believe in marriage stating the "dream of forever is a fairy tale." I loved watching Alexa break through his self-made barriers and bring this hot-blooded, sexy man to his knees. He has lived a life of not feeling wanted and clearly is a lost, tortured soul</span>
  <span id="freeText1006034498925409860" style="display:none">This is a fun, sexy read that I enjoyed...<b>3.5 stars</b><br /><br />Jennifer Probst took the Marriage of Convenience plot and with her witty dialog, the strong build of sexual tension and finally those hot love scenes and made this a winner. <br /><br />Nick Ryan doesn't believe in marriage stating the "dream of forever is a fairy tale." I loved watching Alexa break through his self-made barriers and bring this hot-blooded, sexy man to his knees. He has lived a life of not feeling wanted and clearly is a lost, tortured soul. His life is ruled by logic and reason and is determined to not fall in love.<br /><br />As much as I fell in love with the hero, I loved Alexa as well. There's nothing pretentious about her. She is passionate, open and honest but above all I liked she has backbone. <br /><br />This may be my first read by this author but certainly plan on reading the next book in this series, The Marriage Trap. I'm already intrigued by the heroine, Maggie and partly in love with the Conte.<br /><br /></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1379311007" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16810667407662546865"><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13486122.The_Marriage_Bargain__Marriage_to_a_Billionaire___1_' title='The Marriage Bargain (Marriage to a Billionaire, #1) by Jennifer Probst' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Marriage Bargain</a> is the first installment in <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2965489.Jennifer_Probst' title='Jennifer Probst' rel='nofollow noopener'>Jennifer Probst</a>'s adult contemporary romance series titled <u>Marriage to a Billionaire</u>. I found this little 6-hour audiobook at my local library and decided it would make for some short and sweet entertainment during an afternoon of paperwork. It did just that. <br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13486122.The_Marriage_Bargain__Marriage_to_a_Billionaire___1_' title='The Marriage Bargain (Marriage to a Billionaire, #1) by Jennifer Probst' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Marriage Bargain</a> is pretty superficial, featuring the tried-and-true story of two people agreeing to marry on paper for business, family, etc. while keeping their private interactions non</span>
  <span id="freeText16810667407662546865" style="display:none"><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13486122.The_Marriage_Bargain__Marriage_to_a_Billionaire___1_" title="The Marriage Bargain (Marriage to a Billionaire, #1) by Jennifer Probst" rel="nofollow noopener">The Marriage Bargain</a> is the first installment in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2965489.Jennifer_Probst" title="Jennifer Probst" rel="nofollow noopener">Jennifer Probst</a>'s adult contemporary romance series titled <u>Marriage to a Billionaire</u>. I found this little 6-hour audiobook at my local library and decided it would make for some short and sweet entertainment during an afternoon of paperwork. It did just that. <br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13486122.The_Marriage_Bargain__Marriage_to_a_Billionaire___1_" title="The Marriage Bargain (Marriage to a Billionaire, #1) by Jennifer Probst" rel="nofollow noopener">The Marriage Bargain</a> is pretty superficial, featuring the tried-and-true story of two people agreeing to marry on paper for business, family, etc. while keeping their private interactions non-emotional and non-sexual. Of course, this fictional plan always fails, but it's pretty hot to watch these characters grow increasingly attracted to each other while desperately trying not to. Even though this theme never seems to grow old for me, I didn't find <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13486122.The_Marriage_Bargain__Marriage_to_a_Billionaire___1_" title="The Marriage Bargain (Marriage to a Billionaire, #1) by Jennifer Probst" rel="nofollow noopener">The Marriage Bargain</a> to be crazy good compared to some of the others I have read. Yes, it was an enjoyable read overall, but I don't feel any urgency to search for the other installments. However, I would consider continuing the series via audio on heavy paperwork days when paying close attention to every word isn't a necessity. <br /><br />If you're like me and are looking for a fairly brief and simple romance to pass the time, then this should do the trick. Check it out!<br /><br /><b>My favorite quote:</b><br /><i>"Marriage is messy. People make mistakes. Sometimes we do terrible things, but the vows you've spoken encompass good times and bad."</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="16810667407662546865" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
