<div id="review_435888006" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/435888006" />
    <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog"><img alt="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1429608146p2/12994342.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/435888006?book_show_action=true">Oct 17, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog">Smitten&#39;s Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer435888006" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14736479641490977429"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394574i/759700._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394574i/759701._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>A quick, easy read. This book didn't rock my world but it was pleasant and undemanding. A nice blend of tension, angst, wit, romance, love and steam.<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Hell, at this rate she’d end up in the mental institution by the end of the year. <br/>Cause: Celibacy.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>There weren't any rip-your-heart-out moments for me but I loved the building sexual tension and the avoiding of the inevitable. <br/><br/>I felt that the book would have benefited from a little more depth to take it up a notch, from good to great, and</span>
  <span id="freeText14736479641490977429" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394574i/759700._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394574i/759701._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>A quick, easy read. This book didn't rock my world but it was pleasant and undemanding. A nice blend of tension, angst, wit, romance, love and steam.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Hell, at this rate she’d end up in the mental institution by the end of the year. <br>Cause: Celibacy.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>There weren't any rip-your-heart-out moments for me but I loved the building sexual tension and the avoiding of the inevitable. <br><br>I felt that the book would have benefited from a little more depth to take it up a notch, from good to great, and the characters were a little one dimensional. I felt that some of the book seemed a little rushed and I would have enjoyed reading more about their day to day life, getting to know one another, etc. etc.<br><br>I didn't fall head over heels in love with the characters, although I did like them and I didn't find myself banging my head against any brick walls.<br><br>The ending is cute and development of Nick's character is quite heart warming. But, I have to say, it is very predictable.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“It's always been you. I don't want anybody else; I don't dream about anybody else. It's only you.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>If you aren't looking for anything too taxing or emotional, it's a fun, simple read.<br><br>To read more reviews go to my Book Blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/">http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/</a><br>Follow me on Twitter: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://twitter.com/SmittenSC">https://twitter.com/SmittenSC</a><br>Find me on Pinterest: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://pinterest.com/smittensc/">http://pinterest.com/smittensc/</a><br>Join in the chat on Facebook: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/groups/427743250626754/?fref=ts">http://www.facebook.com/groups/427743...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="14736479641490977429" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('AioPhRf9MePkUSaIPsIUgSJkgR3NAKxN39M5pR3XUhvUHNCp+1bOur+Y8q5MHV09AgdPuRp22RpzlORdOGPvEQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('xiz6U8Zu2ZCfCIF6BEZ1jnYLr42JpSj8uqsZsuDFI5cQGiV/KsUmycTBVVx2mTwyVmhhKV7TXasW7MRKxXGenQ==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<span id="freeTextContainer1046432538593383452">Jennifer Probst wrote her first book at twelve years old. She bound it in a folder, read it to her classmates, and hasn’t stopped writing since. She took a short hiatus to get married, get pregnant, buy a house, get pregnant again, pursue a master’s in English Literature, and rescue two shelter dogs. Now she is writing again.<br/> <br/>She is the NYT, USA Today, and Wall Street Journal bestselling author of</span>
  <span id="freeText1046432538593383452" style="display:none">Jennifer Probst wrote her first book at twelve years old. She bound it in a folder, read it to her classmates, and hasn’t stopped writing since. She took a short hiatus to get married, get pregnant, buy a house, get pregnant again, pursue a master’s in English Literature, and rescue two shelter dogs. Now she is writing again.<br /> <br />She is the NYT, USA Today, and Wall Street Journal bestselling author of sexy and erotic contemporary romance. She was thrilled her book, The Marriage Bargain, was ranked #6 on Amazon's Best Books for 2012, and spent 26 weeks on the NY Times. Her work has been translated in over a dozen countries, sold over a million copies, and was dubbed a "romance phenom" by Kirkus Reviews. She loves hearing from readers. Visit her website for updates on new releases and her street team at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.jenniferprobst.com">www.jenniferprobst.com</a>. Sign up of her newsletter at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.jenniferprobst.com/newsletter">www.jenniferprobst.com/newsletter</a> for a chance to win a free book and receive exclusive material and giveaways.<br /></span>
